msg:Kaiyuan Mingdu Hotel, located at No. 278 Renmin East Road, Yuecheng District, Shaoxing, should be one of the earlier five-star hotels in Shaoxing City. It has a superior geographical location and convenient transportation. Especially during the Chinese New Year, the bus and scenic spots are free. The business is super hot, and the check-in and check-out are super fast. But the buffet breakfast is a bit regrettable. There are too many people and the supply is insufficient. There is a lot of bacon and my husband got a cold one. There are too few varieties of Western food! Chinese food is OK.
Room facilities: The luxury floor is high, the washbasin is spacious, the bathtub is very large, and the bedroom is too small. There are not many sockets. The bath and shampoo products are good, but there is no skin care shower cap, and the wifi card. The waiter has a good attitude.
2 tickets for the night tour of the city river: It is also worth a visit!
In short, it is still a little short of five stars.
